# Classification of Handwritten Digits


```R
library(MASS)
train_input<-read.csv('trainInput.csv',header=F)
train_output<-read.csv('trainOutput.csv',header=F)
test_input<-read.csv('testInput.csv',header=F)
test_output<- read.csv('testoutput.csv', header = F)
```


```R
As <- list()
for ( i in 0:9) {
    As[[i+1]] <- t(train_input[ ,which(train_output[1,] == i)])
}
```


```R
svd <- list()
```


```R
for(j in 1:10) {
    A <-  As[[j]]
    svd <- svd(A)
}
```


```R
A <- list()
```


```R
for (j in 1:10){
    A[[j]] <- svd(As[[j]], nv = 20)$v
}
```

A

```R
b <- c()
for (j in 1:ncol(test_input)){
    Error0 = norm(A[[1]] %*% (ginv(A[[1]]) %*% test_input[,j]) - test_input[,j], '2')
    result = c(Error0)
    preds = result - 1 
    b = append(b, preds) 
    j=j+1
}
```

l <- mean(b == as.numeric(test_output[1,]))
